                                    status: 1,
                                    msg: 'SSR Entry'

                                    window['NanoInitStage']['SSR_NanoInstance'] = {
                                        status: 0,
                                        msg: 'nano instance is undefined in ssr created context'
                                    }

                                    window['NanoInitStage']['SSR_NanoInstance'] = {
                                        status: 1,
                                        msg: 'nano instance is defined in ssr created context'
                                    }
                                    function gqs(name) {
                                        var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)");
                                        var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
                                        if (r != null) {
                                            return unescape(r[2])
                                        }
                                        return null
                                    }
                                    function connectPlayer() {
                                        if (vd && vd.aid) {
                                            if (vd.embedPlayer) {
                                                if (typeof window.performance !== 'undefined' && typeof window.performance.timing !== 'undefined') {
                                                    performance.timing.embedPlayer = Date.now()
                                                }
                                                var fp = gqs('p') || gqs('page') || null
                                                var p = fp ? fp - 1 : 0
                                                var playerInfo = {
                                                    aid: vd.aid,
                                                    bvid: vd.bvid,
                                                    cid: (vd.pages[p] && vd.pages[p].cid) || vd.pages[0].cid,
                                                    p: p + 1,
                                                    t: gqs('t') || 0,
                                                    fromDid: gqs('dmid'),
                                                }
                                                var featureList = new Set(['blackGap'])
                                                var stats = {
                                                    spmId: '333.788.0.0',
                                                    spmIdFrom: gqs('spm_id_from') || '',
                                                }
                                                var theme = {
                                                    'bpx-primary-color': 'var(--brand_blue)',
                                                    'bpx-fn-color': 'var(--brand_blue)',
                                                    'bpx-fn-hover-color': 'var(--brand_blue)',

                                                    'bpx-aux-float-icon': 'var(--graph_icon)',
                                                    'bpx-aux-block-icon': 'var(--text3)',
                                                    'bpx-dmsend-info-font': 'var(--text2)',

                                                    'bpx-aux-header-font': 'var(--text1)',

                                                    'bpx-aux-footer-font-hover': 'var(--text1)',
                                                    'bpx-aux-content-font1': 'var(--text1)',
                                                    'bpx-aux-content-font2': 'var(--text2)',
                                                    'bpx-aux-content-font3': 'var(--text2)',
                                                    'bpx-aux-content-font4': 'var(--text3)',
                                                    'bpx-aux-content-font5': 'var(--text3)',
                                                    'bpx-dmsend-main-bg': 'var(--bg1)',
                                                    'bpx-dmsend-input-bg': 'var(--bg3)',
                                                    'bpx-aux-header-bg': 'var(--graph_bg_regular)',

                                                    'bpx-aux-content-bg': 'var(--bg1)',

                                                }
                                                var primarySetting = {
                                                    element: document.getElementById('bilibili-player'),
                                                    auxiliary: document.querySelector('.danmaku-wrap'),
                                                    aid: playerInfo.aid,
                                                    cid: playerInfo.cid,
                                                    bvid: playerInfo.bvid,
                                                    p: playerInfo.p,
                                                    t: playerInfo.t,
                                                    fromDid: playerInfo.fromDid,
                                                    kind: nano.GroupKind.Ugc,

                                                    stats: stats,
                                                    enableHEVC: true,
                                                    enableAV1: true,
                                                    enableWMP: true,
                                                    revision: 1,
                                                }

                                                        playUrl: window.__playinfo__
                                                    }
                                                }
                                                if (playerInfo.fromDid) {
                                                    primarySetting.autoplay = true
                                                }
                                                window.player = nano.createPlayer(primarySetting, theme)
                                                window.player.connect()
                                                window.isEmbedPlayer = true
                                            } else if (vd.embed) {
                                                document.querySelector("#bilibili-player").innerHTML = vd.embed
                                            }
                                        }
